### [97] [Stable but Wrong: An Inference Limit in Galactic Archaeology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27368)
*Zhipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现，在银河考古学中，恒星年龄推断的观测质量（信噪比和视差精度）可能会引入系统性偏差，导致推断结果在统计上稳定但实际错误（偏差0.5-1 Gyr），挑战了“大数据带来更可靠结论”的传统假设。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 挑战观测科学中“样本量增大→结果收敛到真实值”的传统假设，探究观测质量是否会在银河考古学的年龄推断中引入系统性偏差。

Method: 利用大量亚巨星样本，在观测质量参数空间（信噪比和视差精度）中，识别出推断的形成时标相对于独立星震学参考出现系统性偏移的区域。

Result: 在特定观测质量区域内，推断的银盘形成时标相对于独立星震学参考存在0.5-1 Gyr的系统性偏移，而统计不确定性仍然很小，形成“稳定但错误”的推断状态。

Conclusion: 观测质量可能引入系统性偏差，导致看似可靠实则错误的推断结果，表明在观测科学中需要谨慎对待基于大数据的推断结论。

Original Abstract: Statistical inference in observational science typically relies on a fundamental assumption: as sample size increases and uncertainties decrease, the inferred results should converge to the true physical quantities. This assumption underpins the notion that big data lead to more reliable conclusions. In Galactic archaeology, stellar ages inferred from spectroscopic surveys are widely used to reconstruct the formation history of the Milky Way disk. The age metallicity relation (AMR) and its derived formation timescale are often regarded as key physical diagnostics of early disk evolution. This interpretation carries an implicit premise: that observational quality does not introduce systematic bias into age inference. Here we show that this premise may fail. Using a large sample of subgiant stars, we identify a region in the observational quality parameter space (signal-to-noise ratio and parallax precision) where the inferred formation timescale exhibits a systematic offset of 0.5-1 Gyr relative to an independent asteroseismic reference, while the statistical uncertainties remain small, thus producing a stable-but-wrong inference state.

中文摘要翻译: 观测科学中的统计推断通常依赖于一个基本假设：随着样本量增大和不确定性减小，推断结果应收敛到真实的物理量。这一假设支撑着“大数据带来更可靠结论”的观点。在银河考古学中，从光谱巡天推断出的恒星年龄被广泛用于重建银盘的形成历史。年龄-金属丰度关系（AMR）及其推导出的形成时标常被视为早期银盘演化的关键物理诊断。这种解释蕴含着一个隐含前提：观测质量不会在年龄推断中引入系统性偏差。本文表明，这一前提可能不成立。利用大量亚巨星样本，我们在观测质量参数空间（信噪比和视差精度）中识别出一个区域，在该区域中推断的形成时标相对于独立的星震学参考存在0.5-1 Gyr的系统性偏移，而统计不确定性仍然很小，从而产生了一种“稳定但错误”的推断状态。

</details>


### [98] [Detecting is Easy, Adapting is Hard: Local Expert Growth for Visual Model-Based Reinforcement Learning under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27411)
*Haiyang Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth方法，通过冻结JEPA表示进行问题索引，并添加聚类特定的局部残差专家来修正动作，在不修改基础控制器的情况下显著提升视觉MBRL在分布外场景的性能，同时保留分布内性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 视觉MBRL智能体在训练分布上表现良好，但测试环境发生偏移时性能下降。现有方法难以在检测到偏移后有效进行动作层面的修正，要么无法改进闭环控制，要么会损害分布内性能。

Method: 提出JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth方法：使用冻结的JEPA表示仅用于问题索引，聚类特定的残差专家在原始控制器之上添加局部动作修正，而不修改基础控制器本身。通过paired-bootstrap评估，采用harder-pair变体来增强稳定性。

Result: harder-pair变体在所有四种偏移条件下均产生统计显著的分布外性能提升，同时保留分布内性能。学习的专家在再次遇到相同偏移时仍然有效，支持适应是增量知识增长而非重复完整重训练的观点。简单密度模型可实现自动分布内拒绝，但细粒度分布外子类区分受限于表示能力。

Conclusion: 视觉MBRL在分布偏移下的主要挑战不是检测环境变化，而是在识别变化后施加正确的局部动作修正。

Original Abstract: Visual model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agents can perform well on the training distribution, but often break down once the test environment shifts. In visual MBRL, recognizing that a shift has occurred is often the easier part; the harder part is turning that recognition into useful action-level correction. We study several ways of responding to shift, including planning penalties, direct fine-tuning, global residual correction, and coarse gating. In our experiments, these approaches either do not improve closed-loop control or hurt in-distribution (ID) performance. Based on these negative results, we propose JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth. The method uses a frozen JEPA representation only for problem indexing, while cluster-specific residual experts add local action corrections on top of the original controller. The baseline controller itself is not modified. Using paired-bootstrap evaluation, we find that the original naive-preference variant is not stable under stricter testing. In contrast, the harder-pair variant produces statistically significant OOD improvements on all four evaluated shift conditions while preserving ID performance. The learned experts also remain useful when the same shift is encountered again, which supports the view of adaptation as incremental knowledge growth rather than repeated full retraining. We further show that automatic ID rejection can be achieved with simple density models, whereas fine-grained discrimination among OOD sub-families is limited by the representation. Overall, the results indicate that, for visual MBRL under distribution shift, the main challenge is not simply noticing that the environment has changed, but applying the right local action correction after the change has been recognized.

中文摘要翻译: 基于视觉的模型强化学习（MBRL）智能体在训练分布上可以表现良好，但一旦测试环境发生偏移，性能往往会崩溃。在视觉MBRL中，识别出偏移已经发生通常是较容易的部分；较难的部分是将这种识别转化为有用的动作层面修正。我们研究了多种应对偏移的方法，包括规划惩罚、直接微调、全局残差修正和粗粒度门控。在我们的实验中，这些方法要么不能改进闭环控制，要么会损害分布内性能。基于这些负面结果，我们提出了JEPA索引的局部专家增长方法。该方法仅使用冻结的JEPA表示进行问题索引，同时聚类特定的残差专家在原始控制器之上添加局部动作修正。基线控制器本身不被修改。通过配对自助法评估，我们发现原始朴素偏好变体在更严格的测试下并不稳定。相比之下，更难配对变体在所有四种评估的偏移条件下均产生统计显著的分布外改进，同时保留分布内性能。学习的专家在再次遇到相同偏移时仍然有效，这支持了将适应视为增量知识增长而非重复完整重训练的观点。我们进一步证明，使用简单密度模型可以实现自动分布内拒绝，而分布外子类之间的细粒度区分受限于表示能力。总体而言，结果表明，对于分布偏移下的视觉MBRL，主要挑战不仅仅是注意到环境已经改变，而是在识别变化后应用正确的局部动作修正。

### [99] [ChipLingo: A Systematic Training Framework for Large Language Models in EDA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27415)
*Lei Li,Xingwen Yu,Jianguo Ni,Junxuan Zhu,Jieqiong Zhang,Jian Zhao,Zhi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ChipLingo，一种面向EDA领域的LLM系统化训练流程，通过领域语料构建、领域自适应预训练和指令对齐三阶段训练，显著提升了LLM在EDA任务上的性能，ChipLingo-32B达到70.02%准确率，接近闭源商业模型。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: EDA领域知识密集、文档驱动，通用LLM直接应用面临领域专业知识不足、跨工具知识混淆以及领域训练后检索增强生成（RAG）性能下降等问题。

Method: ChipLingo包含三个阶段：(1) 领域语料构建：多源数据整理与问答增强；(2) 领域自适应预训练：比较不同参数训练策略；(3) 指令对齐：在多样化检索条件下进行RAG场景训练。同时构建了内部基准EDA-Bench。

Result: ChipLingo-8B在EDA-Bench上达到59.7%准确率，优于同规模基础模型和部分大型通用模型；ChipLingo-32B达到70.02%，接近闭源商业模型。分析表明：QA增强提升领域性能，Partial FT比LoRA更好平衡领域适应与通用能力，显式RAG场景训练缓解了领域训练后检索利用率下降问题。

Conclusion: 系统化的领域训练对知识密集型EDA任务具有实用价值，为未来EDA智能体和外部知识驱动系统奠定了基础。

Original Abstract: With the rapid advancement of semiconductor technology, Electronic Design Automation (EDA) has become an increasingly knowledge-intensive and document-driven engineering domain. Although large language models (LLMs) have shown strong general capabilities, applying them directly to EDA remains challenging due to limited domain expertise, cross-tool knowledge confusion, and degraded retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) performance after domain training. To address these issues, this paper presents ChipLingo, a systematic training pipeline for domain-adapted LLMs tailored to EDA scenarios.

We also curate an internal benchmark, EDA-Bench, covering representative EDA tool scenarios, with plans for public release.

ChipLingo-32B reaches 70.02%, approaching leading closed-source commercial models. Further analysis shows that QA augmentation improves domain performance, Partial FT offers a better balance between adaptation and general capability retention than LoRA, and explicit RAG scenario training mitigates the decline in retrieval utilization after domain training. These results demonstrate the practical value of systematic domain training for knowledge-intensive EDA tasks and provide a foundation for future EDA agents and external-knowledge-driven systems.

中文摘要翻译: 随着半导体技术的快速发展，电子设计自动化（EDA）已成为一个日益知识密集型和文档驱动的工程领域。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）展现了强大的通用能力，但由于领域专业知识有限、跨工具知识混淆以及领域训练后检索增强生成（RAG）性能下降，直接将它们应用于EDA仍面临挑战。针对这些问题，本文提出了ChipLingo，一种面向EDA场景的领域自适应LLM系统化训练流程。ChipLingo包含三个阶段：多源数据整理与问答增强的领域语料构建、不同参数训练策略对比的领域自适应预训练，以及在多样化检索条件下进行指令对齐的RAG场景训练。我们还构建了内部基准EDA-Bench，涵盖代表性EDA工具场景，并计划公开发布。实验表明，ChipLingo-8B在EDA-Bench上达到59.7%的准确率，优于同规模基础模型和部分大型通用模型。ChipLingo-32B达到70.02%，接近领先的闭源商业模型。进一步分析表明，问答增强提升了领域性能，Partial FT比LoRA更好地平衡了领域适应与通用能力保持，显式RAG场景训练缓解了领域训练后检索利用率下降的问题。这些结果证明了系统化领域训练对知识密集型EDA任务的实用价值，并为未来的EDA智能体和外部知识驱动系统奠定了基础。

### [100] [AdaBFL: Multi-Layer Defensive Adaptive Aggregation for Bzantine-Robust Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27434)
*Zehui Tang,Yuchen Liu,Feihu Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于三层防御机制的自适应聚合方法AdaBFL，用于联邦学习中抵御拜占庭攻击，在非凸非独立同分布设定下具有收敛保证，实验证明优于现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有拜占庭鲁棒方法难以在多种攻击类型间提供平衡防御，或依赖于服务器拥有数据集，为解决这些缺陷，需要一种无需服务器数据集且能自适应调整防御权重的多类型攻击防御方法。

Method: 提出AdaBFL，基于新颖的三层防御机制实现自适应聚合：能够根据攻击类型动态调整防御算法的权重，从而有效应对复杂攻击场景。

Result: 在多个数据集上的综合实验表明，AdaBFL在防御性能上优于对比算法；同时在非凸非独立同分布数据设定下证明了收敛性。

Original Abstract: Federated learning (FL) is a popular distributed learning paradigm in machine learning, which enables multiple clients to collaboratively train models under the guidance of a server without exposing private client data. To counter such attacks, although various Byzantine-robust methods have been proposed, these methods struggle to provide balanced defense against multiple types of attacks or rely on possessing the dataset in the server. To deal with these drawbacks, thus, we propose an effective multi-layer defensive adaptive aggregation for Bzantine-robust federated learning (AdaBFL) based on a novel three-layer defensive mechanism, which can adaptively adjust the weights of defense algorithms to counter complex attacks. 中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习（FL）是机器学习中一种流行的分布式学习范式，它使得多个客户端能够在服务器的指导下协同训练模型，而无需暴露客户端私有数据。然而，FL的去中心化特性使其容易遭受投毒攻击，恶意客户端可能提交被破坏的模型来操纵系统。为了应对此类攻击，尽管已有多种拜占庭鲁棒方法被提出，但这些方法难以在多种攻击类型之间提供平衡的防御，或者依赖于服务器拥有数据集。为了解决这些缺陷，我们提出了一种基于新颖三层防御机制的有效多层防御自适应聚合方法——拜占庭鲁棒联邦学习（AdaBFL），该方法能够自适应调整防御算法的权重以应对复杂攻击。此外，我们还提供了在非独立同分布数据上的非凸设定下AdaBFL方法的收敛性质。跨多个数据集的综合实验验证了AdaBFL相较于可比算法的优越性。

### [101] [ABC: Any-Subset Autoregression via Non-Markovian Diffusion Bridges in Continuous Time and Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27443)
*Gabe Guo,Thanawat Sornwanee,Lutong Hao,Elon Litman,Stefano Ermon,Jose Blanchet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ABC框架，通过连续时间与空间中的非马尔可夫扩散桥实现任意子集自回归建模，用于生成条件连续时空随机过程（如视频、天气预报），解决了现有扩散模型在结构相似性、时间敏感性和任意子集条件约束方面的三大局限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有扩散模型在生成连续时空随机过程时存在三个关键局限：(1) 噪声到数据的演化过程无法捕捉物理时间上邻近状态之间的结构相似性，且在低步数情况下积分不稳定；(2) 注入的随机噪声对物理过程的时间流逝不敏感，导致动态生成不正确；(3) 忽略了基于状态任意子集（如不规则采样时间步、未来观测）的条件约束。

Method: 提出ABC框架，用一个连续的随机微分方程（SDE）对整个物理过程建模，其时间变量和中间状态跟踪真实物理时间和过程状态。通过路径空间上的测度变换推导SDE动力学，并推导出路径和时间依赖的去噪分数匹配方法用于学习这些动力学。核心创新包括：以接近的前一状态而非无信息噪声作为生成起点、随机噪声注入与物理时间流逝成比例缩放、支持路径依赖的任意子集条件约束。

Result: 在视频生成和天气预报等多个领域上的实验表明，ABC方法优于现有的竞争方法。

Conclusion: ABC框架通过连续时空中的非马尔可夫扩散桥，有效解决了现有扩散模型在条件连续时空过程生成中的三大局限性，并取得了显著优越的实验表现。

Original Abstract: Generating continuous-time, continuous-space stochastic processes (e.g., videos, weather forecasts) conditioned on partial observations (e.g., first and last frames) is a fundamental challenge. Existing approaches, (e.g., diffusion models), suffer from key limitations: (1) noise-to-data evolution fails to capture structural similarity between states close in physical time and has unstable integration in low-step regimes; (2) random noise injected is insensitive to the physical process's time elapsed, resulting in incorrect dynamics; (3) they overlook conditioning on arbitrary subsets of states (e.g., irregularly sampled timesteps, future observations). We propose ABC: Any-Subset Autoregressive Models via Non-Markovian Diffusion Bridges in Continuous Time and Space. Crucially, we model the process with one continual SDE whose time variable and intermediate states track the real time and process states. This has provable advantages: (1) the starting point for generating future states is the already-close previous state, rather than uninformative noise; (2) random noise injection scales with physical time elapsed, encouraging physically plausible dynamics with similar time-adjacent states. We derive SDE dynamics via changes-of-measure on path space, yielding another advantage: (3) path-dependent conditioning on arbitrary subsets of the state history and/or future. To learn these dynamics, we derive a path- and time-dependent extension of denoising score matching. Our experiments show ABC's superiority to competing methods on multiple domains, including video generation and weather forecasting.

中文摘要翻译: 生成以部分观测（如首帧和末帧）为条件的连续时间、连续空间随机过程（例如视频、天气预报）是一项基本挑战。现有方法（如扩散模型）存在关键局限性：(1) 噪声到数据的演化无法捕捉物理时间上邻近状态间的结构相似性，且在低步数情况下积分不稳定；(2) 注入的随机噪声对物理过程的时间流逝不敏感，导致动态生成不正确；(3) 忽视了基于状态任意子集（例如不规则采样时间步、未来观测）的条件约束。我们提出ABC：基于连续时间与空间中非马尔可夫扩散桥的任意子集自回归模型。关键在于，我们用一个连续的随机微分方程（SDE）对整个物理过程建模，其时间变量和中间状态跟踪真实的物理时间和过程状态。这具有可证明的优势：(1) 生成未来状态的起点是已经接近的前一状态，而非无信息噪声；(2) 随机噪声注入与物理时间流逝成比例缩放，鼓励生成具有物理合理动态的、时间上相邻相似的状态。我们通过路径空间上的测度变换推导出SDE动力学，从而获得另一优势：(3) 路径依赖的、基于状态历史（和/或未来）的任意子集条件约束。为学习这些动力学，我们推导了一种路径和时间依赖的扩展去噪分数匹配方法。实验表明，ABC在多个领域（包括视频生成和天气预报）优于竞争方法。

### [102] [Improving Graph Few-shot Learning with Hyperbolic Space and Denoising Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27462)
*Yonghao Liu,Jialu Sun,Wei Pang,Fausto Giunchiglia,Ximing Li,Xiaoyue Feng,Renchu Guan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出IMPRESS框架，通过双曲空间表示学习和去噪扩散机制，解决图少样本学习中欧氏空间无法捕捉层次结构以及少样本导致的目标分布偏差问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有图少样本学习方法在元训练阶段使用欧氏空间进行节点表示学习，难以捕捉真实图数据中的层次结构；在元测试阶段仅基于少量支持样本拟合经验目标分布，与真实分布存在显著偏差。

Method: 提出IMPRESS框架：1）在双曲空间中进行节点表示学习以捕捉层次结构；2）利用去噪扩散机制丰富支持分布，缓解少样本导致的分布偏差问题。

Result: 理论上，IMPRESS实现了更紧的泛化界；实验上，在多个基准数据集上一致优于竞争基线方法。

Conclusion: 双曲空间表示学习与去噪扩散机制的结合能有效提升图少样本学习的性能，在理论和实验层面均展现出优势。

Original Abstract: Graph few-shot learning, which focuses on effectively learning from only a small number of labeled nodes to quickly adapt to new tasks, has garnered significant research attention. Despite recent advances in graph few-shot learning that have demonstrated promising performance, existing methods still suffer from several key limitations. First, during the meta-training phase, these methods typically perform node representation learning in Euclidean space, which often fails to capture the inherently hierarchical structure existing in real-world graph data. Second, during the meta-testing phase, they usually fit an empirical target distribution derived from only a few support samples, even when this distribution significantly deviates from the true underlying distribution. To address these issues, we propose IMPRESS, a novel framework that IMproves graPh few-shot learning with hypeRbolic spacE and denoiSing diffuSion. Specifically, our model learns node representations in a hyperbolic space and enriches the support distribution through denoising diffusion mechanisms. Theoretically, IMPRESS achieves a tighter generalization bound. Empirically, IMPRESS consistently outperforms competitive baselines across multiple benchmark datasets.

中文摘要翻译: 图少样本学习专注于如何从仅有的少量标记节点中有效学习以快速适应新任务，该方向已获得大量研究关注。尽管近年来图少样本学习方法取得了令人瞩目的性能，现有方法仍存在若干关键局限。首先，在元训练阶段，这些方法通常在欧氏空间中进行节点表示学习，这往往无法捕捉真实图数据中固有的层次结构。其次，在元测试阶段，它们通常拟合仅由少量支持样本推导出的经验目标分布，即使该分布与真实潜在分布存在显著偏差。为解决这些问题，我们提出IMPRESS——一个利用双曲空间与去噪扩散来改进图少样本学习的新框架。具体而言，我们的模型在双曲空间中学习节点表示，并通过去噪扩散机制丰富支持分布。理论上，IMPRESS实现了更紧的泛化界。实验上，IMPRESS在多个基准数据集上一致优于竞争基线方法。

</details>


### [103] [FMCL: Class-Aware Client Clustering with Foundation Model Representations for Heterogeneous Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27510)
*Mahad Ali,Laura J. Brattain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FMCL，一种基于预训练基础模型的一次性类感知客户端聚类框架，通过类级嵌入原型构建语义签名，在不增加通信开销的前提下提升异构联邦学习性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有聚类联邦学习方法依赖原始数据统计量、模型参数或启发式相似度度量，无法捕获跨异构域数据的类级语义结构，且常需迭代协调，通信与计算开销大。

Method: 利用冻结的基础模型为每个客户端计算类级嵌入原型，构建语义客户端签名；通过类感知表示间的余弦距离度量客户端相似性；在训练开始前一次性完成聚类，后续联邦优化过程无需额外通信，且与下游模型架构无关。

Result: 在多个异构基准上的大量实验表明，与非独立同分布数据划分下的现有聚类方法相比，FMCL提升了联邦学习性能，并表现出更稳定的聚类行为。

Conclusion: FMCL通过类级语义签名实现一次性聚类，有效解决了统计异构性下的联邦学习性能退化问题，兼具高效性与架构无关性。

Original Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training across distributed clients without sharing raw data, yet its performance deteriorates under statistical heterogeneity. Clustered Federated Learning addresses this challenge by grouping similar clients and training separate models per cluster. However, existing clustering strategies often rely on raw data statistics, model parameters, or heuristic similarity measures that fail to capture class-level semantic structure across heterogeneous domains and frequently require iterative coordination. We propose FMCL, a one-shot, class-aware client clustering framework that leverages foundation model representations to construct semantic client signatures. Using a frozen foundation model, FMCL computes class-level embedding prototypes for each client and measures similarity via cosine distance between their class-aware representations. Clustering is performed once prior to training, introducing no additional communication during federated optimization and remaining agnostic to the downstream model architecture. Extensive experiments across heterogeneous benchmarks demonstrate that FMCL improves federated performance and yields more stable clustering behavior compared to existing clustering-based methods under non-identically distributed data partitioning.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习能够在分布式客户端之间无需共享原始数据即可协作训练模型，但其性能在统计异构性下会显著退化。聚类联邦学习通过将相似客户端分组并为每个簇训练单独模型来应对这一挑战。然而，现有聚类策略通常依赖于原始数据统计量、模型参数或启发式相似度度量，这些方法无法捕获跨异构域的类级语义结构，且往往需要迭代协调。我们提出FMCL，一种一次性、类感知的客户端聚类框架，利用基础模型表示构建语义客户端签名。FMCL使用冻结的基础模型为每个客户端计算类级嵌入原型，并通过其类感知表示之间的余弦距离度量相似性。聚类在训练开始前一次性完成，在联邦优化过程中不引入额外通信，且与下游模型架构无关。在异构基准上的大量实验表明，与非独立同分布数据划分下的现有聚类方法相比，FMCL提升了联邦学习性能，并表现出更稳定的聚类行为。

### [104] [Diagnosing Capability Gaps in Fine-Tuning Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27547)
*Saeid Asgari Taghanaki,Rakshanda Agarwal,Bruce Sun,Rohan Jha,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Sara Malvar,Rui Ying,Yifei Xu,Guilherme Potje,Tusher Chakraborty,Leonardo de Oliveira Nunes,Ranveer Chandra,Emre Kiciman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GoalCover是一个用于在微调前系统检测大型语言模型训练数据集中能力短板的框架，通过交互式目标分解和自动化覆盖评估，帮助实践者识别并弥补数据集中缺失的能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 微调大型语言模型需要覆盖目标能力的训练数据集，但实践者难以在昂贵的微调运行前识别出数据集在哪些能力上存在短板，这一问题尚未得到有效解决。

Method: GoalCover引导实践者将高层目标结构化分解为原子化、可独立评估的子目标；为每个训练样本计算基于LLM的每个子目标对齐分数；通过低分样本解释的自动分析来揭示缺失的能力。

Result: 在三个领域（医疗问答、法律摘要、代码生成）的受控污染实验中，目标子目标平均下降25.6%，而非目标子目标仅下降2.1%（Cohen's d=1.24）。在金融摘要RFT任务中，使用GoalCover过滤后的数据训练将LLM裁判奖励从3.77提升至4.12（满分5分），结合目标条件合成样本后达到最佳结果4.20。

Conclusion: GoalCover是一种实用的微调前诊断工具，能够检测能力短板并产生具体的弥补信号，在两个互补维度的验证中均表现出可靠性和有效性。

Original Abstract: Fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) for domain-specific tasks requires training datasets that comprehensively cover the target capabilities a practitioner needs. Yet identifying which capabilities a dataset fails to support, and doing so before an expensive fine-tuning run, remains a largely unsolved problem. We introduce GoalCover, a framework that helps practitioners systematically detect capability gaps in fine-tuning datasets through interactive goal decomposition and automated coverage assessment. GoalCover guides a practitioner through structured decomposition of a high-level goal into atomic, independently evaluable subgoals; assigns each training sample an LLM-based alignment score against every subgoal; and surfaces missing capabilities through automated analysis of low-scoring sample explanations. We validate the framework along two complementary axes. First, through controlled corruption experiments across three domains (medical QA, legal summarization, code generation), we show that GoalCover reliably distinguishes targeted from non-targeted capability impacts: target subgoals degrade by 25.6% on average versus 2.1% for non-target subgoals (Cohen's d=1.24). Second, we demonstrate downstream utility on a financial-summarization Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT) task with Qwen-3-14B: training on GoalCover-filtered data improves the LLM-judge reward from 3.77 to 4.12 (out of 5) over the unfiltered baseline, and combining filtered data with goal-conditioned synthetic samples yields the strongest result (4.20). The two results together show that GoalCover works as a practical pre-fine-tuning diagnostic: it detects capability gaps and produces concrete signal for closing them.

中文摘要翻译: 针对特定领域任务微调大型语言模型（LLM）时，需要训练数据集全面覆盖实践者所需的目标能力。然而，在昂贵的微调运行之前识别数据集在哪些能力上存在短板，仍然是一个基本未解决的问题。我们提出了GoalCover，一个通过交互式目标分解和自动化覆盖评估来帮助实践者系统检测微调数据集中能力短板的框架。GoalCover引导实践者将高层目标结构化分解为原子化、可独立评估的子目标；为每个训练样本计算基于LLM的每个子目标对齐分数；并通过低分样本解释的自动分析来揭示缺失的能力。我们从两个互补的维度验证了该框架。首先，在三个领域（医疗问答、法律摘要、代码生成）的受控污染实验中，我们证明GoalCover能够可靠地区分目标和非目标的能力影响：目标子目标平均下降25.6%，而非目标子目标仅下降2.1%（Cohen's d=1.24）。其次，我们在一个金融摘要的强化微调（RFT）任务中使用Qwen-3-14B模型展示了下游实用性：在GoalCover过滤后的数据上训练，LLM裁判奖励从无过滤基线的3.77提升至4.12（满分5分），而将过滤数据与目标条件合成样本相结合则取得了最强结果（4.20）。这两个结果共同表明，GoalCover是一种实用的微调前诊断工具：它能够检测能力短板，并产生用于弥补这些短板的切实信号。

### [105] [Beyond the Training Distribution: Mapping Generalization Boundaries in Neural Program Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27551)
*Henrik Voigt,Michael Habeck,Joachim Giesen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过基于领域特定算术语法的严格受控程序合成环境，系统评估了Transformer模型的泛化能力。研究发现，优化密度泛化（多样采样）能提升分布外泛化，但模型在语法新颖性外推任务上性能下降超过30%，且计算扩展带来的收益呈对数线性关系，表明需要新的搜索方法突破瓶颈。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有大规模Transformer在程序合成基准上表现优异，但数据污染和不透明的训练语料库掩盖了其真实泛化能力，无法判断模型是在真正泛化还是仅检索记忆模板。

Method: 构建基于领域特定算术语法的严格受控程序合成环境，系统枚举评估数百万个唯一程序，构建可解释的句法和语义度量空间，精确映射数据分布并采样训练/测试分割以隔离特定分布偏移。

Result: 1) 优化密度泛化（语义和句法空间多样采样）可诱导鲁棒的分布外泛化；2) 支撑泛化评估显示Transformer在外推任务上性能下降超30%；3) 计算扩展与泛化提升呈严格对数线性关系。

Conclusion: 鲁棒泛化需要跨多个流形最大化训练多样性，当前对数线性扩展瓶颈亟需新的基于搜索的方法来突破。

Original Abstract: Large-scale transformers achieve impressive results on program synthesis benchmarks, yet their true generalization capabilities remain obscured by data contamination and opaque training corpora. To rigorously assess whether models are truly generalizing or merely retrieving memorized templates, we introduce a strictly controlled program synthesis environment based on a domain-specific arithmetic grammar. By systematically enumerating and evaluating millions of unique programs, we construct interpretable syntactic and semantic metric spaces. This allows us to precisely map data distributions and sample train and test splits that isolate specific distributional shifts. Our experiments demonstrate that optimizing density generalization -- through diverse sampling over both semantic and syntactic spaces -- induces robust out-of-distribution generalization. Conversely, evaluating support generalization reveals that transformers severely struggle with extrapolation, experiencing a performance drop of over 30% when forced to generate syntactically novel programs. While steadily scaling up compute improves generalization, the gains follow a strictly log-linear relationship. We conclude that robust generalization requires maximizing training diversity across multiple manifolds, and our findings indicate the necessity for novel search-based approaches to break through current log-linear scaling bottlenecks.

中文摘要翻译: 大型Transformer在程序合成基准上取得了令人印象深刻的结果，然而它们真正的泛化能力仍因数据污染和不透明的训练语料库而模糊不清。为了严格评估模型是真正在泛化还是仅仅检索记忆模板，我们引入了一个基于领域特定算术语法的严格受控程序合成环境。通过系统地枚举和评估数百万个唯一程序，我们构建了可解释的句法和语义度量空间。这使得我们能够精确映射数据分布，并采样训练集和测试集分割，以隔离特定的分布偏移。我们的实验表明，优化密度泛化——通过语义和句法空间上的多样采样——能够诱导鲁棒的分布外泛化。相反，评估支撑泛化则揭示了Transformer在外推时严重困难，当被迫生成句法新颖的程序时，性能下降超过30%。虽然稳步增加计算量可以改善泛化，但收益遵循严格的线性对数关系。我们得出结论，鲁棒泛化需要跨多个流形最大化训练多样性，我们的发现表明，需要新的基于搜索的方法来突破当前的对数线性扩展瓶颈。

### [107] [Bayesian policy gradient and actor-critic algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27563)
*Mohammad Ghavamzadeh,Yaakov Engel,Michal Valko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯过程的贝叶斯策略梯度框架，通过将策略梯度建模为高斯过程来减少样本需求并提高梯度估计精度，同时引入基于高斯过程时序差分学习的演员-评论家模型以利用马尔可夫性质，实验表明该方法优于传统蒙特卡洛策略梯度方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统策略梯度方法使用蒙特卡洛技术估计梯度，方差高、样本需求大、收敛慢。本文旨在通过贝叶斯方法降低梯度估计的方差，提高样本效率，并在不增加额外计算成本的情况下提供自然梯度和梯度协方差的不确定性度量。

Method: 首先提出贝叶斯策略梯度框架，将策略梯度建模为高斯过程，将系统轨迹作为基本观测单元。对于马尔可夫系统，进一步提出基于高斯过程时序差分学习的非参数化贝叶斯评论家模型，将动作-价值函数建模为高斯过程，利用贝叶斯规则计算后验分布，并通过合适的策略参数化和先验协方差（核函数）得到期望收益梯度的闭式后验解。

Result: 在多个强化学习问题上的详细实验比较表明，所提出的贝叶斯策略梯度和演员-评论家算法在样本效率和收敛性能上优于经典的基于蒙特卡洛的策略梯度方法。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯策略梯度框架能有效降低梯度估计方差、减少样本需求，并提供自然梯度和不确定性度量；结合贝叶斯评论家模型后能利用马尔可夫性质进一步提升性能。

Original Abstract: Policy gradient methods are reinforcement learning algorithms that adapt a parameterized policy by following a performance gradient estimate. Conventional policy gradient methods use Monte-Carlo techniques to estimate the gradient, which tend to have high variance, requiring many samples and resulting in slow convergence. We first propose a Bayesian framework for policy gradient, based on modeling the policy gradient as a Gaussian process. This reduces the number of samples needed to obtain accurate gradient estimates. Moreover, estimates of the natural gradient and a measure of the uncertainty in the gradient estimates, namely, the gradient covariance, are provided at little extra cost. Since the proposed framework considers system trajectories as its basic observable unit, it does not require the dynamics within trajectories to be of any particular form, and can be extended to partially observable problems. On the downside, it cannot exploit the Markov property when the system is Markovian. To address this, we supplement our Bayesian policy gradient framework with a new actor-critic learning model in which a Bayesian class of non-parametric critics, based on Gaussian process temporal difference learning, is used. Such critics model the action-value function as a Gaussian process, allowing Bayes rule to be used to compute the posterior distribution over action-value functions, conditioned on the observed data. Appropriate choices of the policy parameterization and of the prior covariance (kernel) between action-values yield closed-form expressions for the posterior of the gradient of the expected return with respect to the policy parameters. We perform detailed experimental comparisons of the proposed Bayesian policy gradient and actor-critic algorithms with classic Monte-Carlo based policy gradient methods, on a number of reinforcement learning problems.

中文摘要翻译: 策略梯度方法是一类通过遵循性能梯度估计来调整参数化策略的强化学习算法。传统的策略梯度方法使用蒙特卡洛技术估计梯度，这类方法通常具有高方差，需要大量样本并导致收敛缓慢。我们首先提出一个贝叶斯策略梯度框架，该框架将策略梯度建模为高斯过程。这减少了获得准确梯度估计所需的样本数量。此外，该框架以极小的额外成本提供了自然梯度估计以及梯度估计的不确定性度量（即梯度协方差）。由于所提出的框架将系统轨迹视为基本可观测单元，因此它不要求轨迹内部的动力学具有特定形式，并且可以扩展到部分可观测问题。其缺点在于，当系统具有马尔可夫性时，它无法利用马尔可夫性质。为解决这一问题，我们在贝叶斯策略梯度框架的基础上补充了一种新的演员-评论家学习模型，该模型使用基于高斯过程时序差分学习的贝叶斯非参数化评论家。这类评论家将动作-价值函数建模为高斯过程，从而利用贝叶斯规则在给定观测数据的条件下计算动作-价值函数的后验分布。通过恰当选择策略参数化和动作-价值之间的先验协方差（核函数），可以得到期望收益相对于策略参数的梯度的闭式后验表达式。我们在多个强化学习问题上，将所提出的贝叶斯策略梯度和演员-评论家算法与经典的基于蒙特卡洛的策略梯度方法进行了详细的实验比较。

</details>


### [108] [Learning from a single labeled face and a stream of unlabeled data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27564)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在个人电脑和移动设备身份认证场景中，通常只有用户本人的一张注册图像，且没有其他人的标注数据（缺乏负样本）。现有单样本人脸识别方法假设有多人标注数据，不适用于此场景。本文旨在探索如何利用大量易获取的无标签数据来改善仅有单张正样本时的识别性能。

Method: 将问题形式化为单类分类（one-class classification），提出一种非参数模型学习算法，从一张标注图像（正样本）和一个无标签数据流中学习人脸模型。算法利用无标签数据中蕴含的分布信息来增强对目标类别的建模能力。

Result: 在43人的数据集上，该方法在接近零误报的情况下达到90%的召回率，比最佳基线方法的召回率高出25%以上。此外还进行了全面的敏感性分析，给出了实际应用中的参数设置指南。

Conclusion: 无标签数据可以有效帮助单样本人脸识别这一极具挑战的场景。本文首次系统研究了利用无标签数据改进单样本单人人脸识别问题，实验证明该方法在保持低误报率的同时显著提升了召回率。

Original Abstract: Face recognition from a single image per person is a challenging problem because the training sample is extremely small. We consider a variation of this problem. In our problem, we recognize only one person, and there are no labeled data for any other person. This setting naturally arises in authentication on personal computers and mobile devices, and poses additional challenges because it lacks negative examples. We formalize our problem as one-class classification, and propose and analyze an algorithm that learns a non-parametric model of the face from a single labeled image and a stream of unlabeled data. In many domains, for instance when a person interacts with a computer with a camera, unlabeled data are abundant and easy to utilize. This is the first paper that investigates how these data can help in learning better models in the single-image-per-person setting. Our method is evaluated on a dataset of 43 people and we show that these people can be recognized 90% of time at nearly zero false positives. This recall is 25+% higher than the recall of our best performing baseline. Finally, we conduct a comprehensive sensitivity analysis of our algorithm and provide a guideline for setting its parameters in practice.

中文摘要翻译: 从单张图像进行人脸识别是一个具有挑战性的问题，因为训练样本极其有限。我们考虑了该问题的一个变体：在我们的问题中，仅需识别一个人，且没有任何其他人的标注数据。这种设置自然出现在个人电脑和移动设备的身份认证中，并因缺乏负样本而带来了额外的挑战。我们将该问题形式化为单类分类（one-class classification），并提出并分析了一种算法，该算法从一张标注图像和一个无标签数据流中学习人脸的非参数模型。在许多场景中，例如当用户与带有摄像头的计算机交互时，无标签数据是丰富且易于利用的。本文是首篇研究在单样本单人人脸识别设置下如何利用这些数据来学习更好模型的工作。我们在包含43人的数据集上进行了评估，结果表明，这些人脸可以在接近零误报的情况下以90%的概率被识别。这一召回率比最佳基线方法的召回率高出25%以上。最后，我们对算法进行了全面的敏感性分析，并为其在实际中的参数设置提供了指导。

### [109] [ZAYAN: Disentangled Contrastive Transformer for Tabular Remote Sensing Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27606)
*Al Zadid Sultan Bin Habib,Tanpia Tasnim,Md. Ekramul Islam,Muntasir Tabasum*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ZAYAN是一个面向遥感与环境科学表格数据的自监督特征级对比学习框架，通过零锚点动态特征编码实现冗余最小化的解耦嵌入，在8个数据集上取得优于现有方法的性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 遥感与环境科学中的表格数据存在异质性、标签稀缺和特征冗余问题，现有方法难以有效学习信息丰富的表征。

Method: 提出ZAYAN框架，包含两个模块：ZAYAN-CL通过零锚点对比学习目标结合动态扰动和掩码进行特征嵌入预训练；ZAYAN-T是基于Transformer的分类器，利用预训练的特征嵌入进行下游分类。

Result: 在8个数据集（含6个遥感表格基准和2个洪水预测表格）上，ZAYAN在准确性、鲁棒性和泛化性上均优于表格深度学习方法，在标签稀缺和分布偏移场景下表现一致优异。

Conclusion: 特征级对比学习与动态特征编码为从表格传感数据中学习提供了一种有效方案。

Original Abstract: Learning informative representations from tabular data in remote sensing and environmental science is challenging due to heterogeneity, scarce labels, and redundancy among features. We present ZAYAN (Zero-Anchor dYnamic feAture eNcoding), a self-supervised, feature-centric contrastive framework for tabular data. ZAYAN performs contrastive learning at the feature rather than sample level, removing the need for explicit anchor selection and any reliance on class labels, while encouraging a redundancy-minimized, disentangled embedding space. The framework has two modules: ZAYAN-CL, which pretrains feature embeddings via a zero-anchor contrastive objective with dynamic perturbations and masking, and ZAYAN-T, a Transformer that conditions on these embeddings for downstream classification. Across eight datasets, including six remote-sensing tabular benchmarks and two remote-sensing-driven flood-prediction tables from satellite and GIS products, ZAYAN achieves superior accuracy, robustness, and generalization over tabular deep learning baselines, with consistent gains under label scarcity and distribution shift. These results indicate that feature-level contrastive learning and dynamic feature encoding provide an effective recipe for learning from tabular sensing data.

中文摘要翻译: 从遥感和环境科学的表格数据中学习信息丰富的表征具有挑战性，原因在于数据的异质性、标签稀缺以及特征间的冗余性。我们提出ZAYAN（零锚点动态特征编码），一种面向表格数据的自监督、以特征为中心的对比学习框架。ZAYAN在特征层面而非样本层面执行对比学习，消除了对显式锚点选择和类别标签依赖的需求，同时鼓励构建冗余最小化、解耦的嵌入空间。该框架包含两个模块：ZAYAN-CL通过带有动态扰动和掩码的零锚点对比目标预训练特征嵌入；ZAYAN-T是一个Transformer，基于这些嵌入进行下游分类。在八个数据集上（包括六个遥感表格基准和两个来自卫星与GIS产品的遥感驱动洪水预测表格），ZAYAN在准确性、鲁棒性和泛化性方面均优于表格深度学习基线方法，在标签稀缺和分布偏移条件下保持一致的性能提升。这些结果表明，特征级对比学习和动态特征编码为从表格传感数据中学习提供了一种有效方案。

### [110] [AMGenC: Generating Charge Balanced Amorphous Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27613)
*Yan Lin,Jilin Hu,N. M. Anoop Krishnan,Morten M. Smedskjaer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出AMGenC，一种能保证生成电荷平衡的非晶材料样本的生成式逆向设计方法，通过元素噪声、软投影和离散投影实现，实验验证其有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 非晶材料的生成式逆向设计中，概率生成模型因固有随机性导致大量生成样本电荷不平衡，而现有方法无法有效解决该问题。

Method: 提出AMGenC方法，通过引入元素噪声使生成过程从电荷平衡的起点开始，结合每步软投影和最终离散投影，引导元素在生成过程中始终保持电荷平衡。

Result: 在两个非晶材料数据集上的实验结果表明，AMGenC能够实现其设计目标，即在最小计算开销下保证生成电荷平衡的样本，且不牺牲逆向设计精度。

Conclusion: AMGenC有效解决了非晶材料生成中电荷不平衡的问题，为生成式逆向设计提供了实用且高效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Amorphous (disordered) materials are solids that have shown great potential in various domains, including energy storage, thermal management, and advanced materials. Unlike crystalline materials that can be described by unit cells containing a few to hundreds of atoms, amorphous materials require larger simulation cells with at least hundreds to thousands of atoms. To advance the design of amorphous materials with desired properties and facilitate the exploration of their vast design space, generative inverse design has emerged as a promising approach. It aims to directly output materials with properties closely aligned with the desired ones using probabilistic generative models conditioned on desired properties, which can be more resource efficient than the traditional trial-and-error approach. However, due to the inherent stochasticity of probabilistic generative models, when element assignments are unconstrained, a large portion of generated materials may be charge unbalanced, and no existing methods can effectively mitigate this limitation. In this work, we propose AMGenC, a new generative inverse design method for amorphous materials that can guarantee the generation of charge balanced samples, with minimal additional computational overhead and without sacrificing inverse design accuracy. AMGenC achieves this through an element noise that gives the generation process a starting point centered around charge balance, and the combination of a per-step soft projection and a final discrete projection for steering the elements toward exact charge balance throughout the generation. We perform extensive experiments on two amorphous materials datasets. Experimental results provide evidence that AMGenC achieves its design goal.

中文摘要翻译: 非晶（无序）材料是一种在能量存储、热管理和先进材料等多个领域展现出巨大潜力的固体。与可通过包含几个到数百个原子的单胞来描述的晶体材料不同，非晶材料需要包含至少数百到数千个原子的更大模拟单元。为了推动具有所需特性的非晶材料设计并促进其广阔设计空间的探索，生成式逆向设计已成为一种有前景的方法。它旨在利用以期望属性为条件的概率生成模型，直接输出与目标属性高度匹配的材料，相比传统的试错法更具资源效率。然而，由于概率生成模型固有的随机性，当元素分配不加约束时，生成的材料中很大一部分可能电荷不平衡，而现有方法无法有效缓解这一局限。在这项工作中，我们提出了AMGenC，一种新的非晶材料生成式逆向设计方法，能够在最小额外计算开销且不牺牲逆向设计精度的前提下，保证生成电荷平衡的样本。AMGenC通过引入元素噪声使生成过程从以电荷平衡为中心的起点开始，并结合每步软投影和最终离散投影，在整个生成过程中引导元素走向精确的电荷平衡。我们在两个非晶材料数据集上进行了大量实验，实验结果证明AMGenC实现了其设计目标。

### [112] [ANCORA: Learning to Question via Manifold-Anchored Self-Play for Verifiable Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27644)
*Chengcao Yang,Jun Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ANCORA框架，让语言模型通过自问自答（生成可验证问题并求解）实现无需人类监督的自我改进，在形式化验证任务上将Dafny2Verus pass@1从26.6%提升至81.5%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法依赖人工标注数据或监督信号，探索能否让语言模型自主生成可验证问题、求解并利用反馈进行自我改进，实现完全无监督的自我提升。

Method: ANCORA框架包含三个核心机制：(1) 两级组相对更新，将Proposer的优势与规范（specifications）耦合，Solver的优势与求解尝试耦合；(2) 迭代自蒸馏SFT，先投影到有效输出流形再强化学习；(3) UCB引导的课程DAG，仅通过严格过滤的新颖且可验证的规范来增长。

Result: 在Dafny2Verus基准上，0-shot测试时训练设置下pass@1从26.6%（SFT基线）提升至81.5%，超过PSV自对弈基线15.8个百分点（尽管PSV使用1-shot推理）；迁移设置下在MBPP和HumanEval上分别达到36.2%和17.2%的pass@1。

Conclusion: 验证了语言模型可以通过生成可验证问题并从中学习来实现无监督自我改进，所提出的锚定课程框架和稳定机制是防止策略崩溃的关键。

Original Abstract: We propose a paradigm shift from learning to answer to learning to question: can a language model generate verifiable problems, solve them, and turn the resulting feedback into self-improvement without human supervision? We introduce ANCORA, an anchored-curriculum framework in which a unified policy alternates between a Proposer that synthesizes novel specifications and a Solver that produces verified solutions. ANCORA rests on three load-bearing mechanisms: a two-level group-relative update that couples Proposer advantages across specifications with Solver advantages across solution attempts; iterative self-distilled SFT that projects the base model onto its valid-output manifold before RL; and a UCB-guided Curriculum DAG that grows only through strictly filtered, novel, Solver-verified specifications. These stabilizers are necessary because sparse verifier feedback otherwise drives Proposer collapse even under MLRL-aligned rewards. Instantiated in Verus, ANCORA lifts Dafny2Verus pass@1 from a 26.6% SFT baseline to 81.5% in the test-time-training setting under 0-shot evaluation, outperforming the PSV self-play baseline by 15.8 points despite PSV using 1-shot inference; in a separate transfer setting, training from Dafny2Verus seeds yields 36.2% and 17.2% pass@1 on held-out MBPP and HumanEval.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出从"学习回答"到"学习提问"的范式转变：语言模型能否生成可验证的问题、求解它们、并将由此产生的反馈转化为无需人类监督的自我改进？我们提出了ANCORA，一个锚定课程框架，其中统一策略交替扮演两个角色：生成新颖规范的Proposer和产出已验证解的Solver。ANCORA依赖三个关键稳定机制：两级组相对更新，将Proposer的优势与规范耦合、Solver的优势与求解尝试耦合；迭代自蒸馏SFT，在强化学习之前将基座模型投影到其有效输出流形上；以及UCB引导的课程DAG，仅通过经过严格过滤、新颖且经Solver验证的规范进行增长。这些稳定器是必需的，因为稀疏的验证器反馈即使在多层级强化学习对齐的奖励下也会导致Proposer崩溃。在Verus中实例化的ANCORA，在0-shot评估的测试时训练设置下，将Dafny2Verus pass@1从26.6%的SFT基线提升至81.5%，比PSV自对弈基线高出15.8个百分点，尽管PSV使用了1-shot推理；在另一迁移设置中，从Dafny2Verus种子训练在MBPP和HumanEval上分别取得了36.2%和17.2%的pass@1。

### [113] [Optimized Deferral for Imbalanced Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27723)
*Corinna Cortes,Anqi Mao,Mehryar Mohri,Yutao Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了两阶段学习延迟（Learning to Defer）中的专家不平衡问题，提出基于边际的损失函数与代价敏感学习算法MILD，在图像分类和LLM路由任务上显著优于现有基线。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 两阶段学习延迟设置中，现有预测器（如多个LLM或分类器）存在专家不平衡问题，导致延迟算法偏向多数专家，性能欠佳。现有方法缺乏对此问题的系统性处理。

Method: 将延迟损失优化重新表述为输入-专家域上的新型代价敏感学习问题；推导了针对该设置的基于边际的损失函数及其理论保证；开发了适用于代价敏感学习的新算法，并设计了MILD算法专门处理专家不平衡场景。

Result: 在图像分类和真实世界大语言模型路由任务上进行了大量实验，结果表明MILD方法显著优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 提出的基于边际的不平衡学习延迟算法MILD能有效应对专家不平衡问题，在兼顾准确性与计算成本的同时提升系统整体性能。

Original Abstract: Learning algorithms can be significantly improved by routing complex or uncertain inputs to specialized experts, balancing accuracy with computational cost. This approach, known as learning to defer, is essential in domains like natural language generation, medical diagnosis, and computer vision, where an effective deferral can reduce errors at low extra resource consumption. However, the two-stage learning to defer setting, which leverages existing predictors such as a collection of LLMs or other classifiers, often faces challenges due to an expert imbalance problem. This imbalance can lead to suboptimal performance, with deferral algorithms favoring the majority expert. We present a comprehensive study of two-stage learning to defer in expert imbalance settings. We cast the deferral loss optimization as a novel cost-sensitive learning problem over the input-expert domain. We derive new margin-based loss functions and guarantees tailored to this setting, and develop novel algorithms for cost-sensitive learning. Leveraging these results, we design principled deferral algorithms, MILD (Margin-based Imbalanced Learning to Defer), specifically suited for expert imbalance settings. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach, showing clear improvements over existing baselines on both image classification and real-world Large Language Model (LLM) routing tasks.

中文摘要翻译: 学习算法可以通过将复杂或不确定的输入路由到专门的专家，在准确性与计算成本之间取得平衡，从而得到显著改进。这种方法被称为"学习延迟"（Learning to Defer），在自然语言生成、医学诊断和计算机视觉等领域至关重要，有效的延迟可以在极低的额外资源消耗下减少错误。然而，利用现有预测器（如多个大语言模型或其他分类器集合）的两阶段学习延迟设置，常常面临专家不平衡问题。这种不平衡会导致延迟算法偏向多数专家，从而产生次优性能。本文对专家不平衡场景下的两阶段学习延迟进行了系统性研究。我们将延迟损失优化重新表述为输入-专家域上的新型代价敏感学习问题；推导了针对该设置的基于边际的损失函数及其理论保证，并开发了适用于代价敏感学习的新算法。基于这些成果，我们设计了原则性的延迟算法MILD（基于边际的不平衡学习延迟），专门适用于专家不平衡场景。大量实验证明了我们方法的有效性，在图像分类和真实世界大语言模型路由任务上均显著优于现有基线方法。

### [114] [Differential Subgroup Discovery: Characterizing Where Two Populations Differ, and Why](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27741)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法难以自动识别特征空间中两个群体差异最显著的特定子区域（即差异性子群），而发现这些子群对于揭示群体差异的结构性原因（如临床分析、模型诊断或治疗效果研究）至关重要。

Method: 形式化了差异性子群发现的通用优化目标，建立了子群具备因果解释能力的条件，并提出DiffSub——一种基于梯度的可解释子群发现方法，适用于表格数据。

Result: 在合成基准、医学案例研究、模型误差分析和治疗效果评估等多个场景中，DiffSub能够识别出信息量丰富的子群，有效揭示群体差异产生的位置和原因。

Conclusion: DiffSub能够有效地发现具有因果可解释性的差异性子群，帮助实践者识别导致群体差异的关键协变量组合。

Original Abstract: We study the problem of understanding where two populations differ within a feature space, which we formalize in the concept of a differential subgroup: a subset of individuals from both populations who, despite sharing similar characteristics, exhibit exceptional differences in a target outcome. Differential subgroups reveal the regions of the feature space where population-level gaps are most pronounced and can help practitioners identify the covariate combinations that are structurally responsible for these differences, e.g.~in clinical analysis, model diagnostics, or treatment-effect studies. We introduce a general optimization objective for discovering differential subgroups and establish conditions under which the resulting subgroups admit a causal interpretation of population differences. We propose DiffSub, a gradient-based approach that discovers interpretable differential subgroups in tabular data. Across synthetic benchmarks, medical case studies, model-error analyses, and treatment-effect settings, DiffSub identifies informative subgroups that reveal where population differences arise and why.

中文摘要翻译: 我们研究如何在特征空间中理解两个群体之间的差异，并将其形式化为差异性子群的概念：即来自两个群体的一批个体，尽管具有相似的特征，但在目标结果上表现出显著的差异。差异性子群能够揭示特征空间中群体层面差异最显著的区域，帮助实践者识别在结构上导致这些差异的协变量组合，例如在临床分析、模型诊断或治疗效果研究中的应用。我们引入了一个用于发现差异性子群的通用优化目标，并建立了该子群具有因果解释能力的条件。我们提出DiffSub，一种基于梯度的可解释子群发现方法，适用于表格数据。在合成基准、医学案例研究、模型误差分析和治疗效果评估等多个场景中，DiffSub均能识别出信息丰富的子群，有效揭示群体差异产生的位置及原因。

### [115] [Linear-Core Surrogates: Smooth Loss Functions with Linear Rates for Classification and Structured Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27742)
*Mehryar Mohri,Yutao Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Linear-Core (LC) Surrogates损失函数族，通过将线性核心与平滑尾部拼接，解决了分类中光滑损失（如交叉熵）优化快但统计收敛慢、分段线性损失（如Hinge）统计效率高但不可微的矛盾。该方法在全微分的前提下严格保持线性H-一致性界，并在结构化预测中实现无偏随机梯度估计，避免精确推理的二次复杂度，实验获得23倍加速并对噪声鲁棒。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 分类损失函数存在根本性权衡：光滑损失（如交叉熵）优化速率快但统计收敛速度慢（平方根一致性界），而分段线性损失（如Hinge）统计收敛快（线性一致性界）但不可微，导致优化困难。现有损失函数无法同时兼顾光滑性与统计效率。

Method: 提出Linear-Core (LC) Surrogates，一类新的凸损失函数族。其构造方式是将一个线性核心（linear core）与一个光滑尾部（smooth tail）拼接，使得损失函数处处可微，同时严格保持线性H-一致性界（linear H-consistency bounds）。在结构化预测中，利用光滑性构建无偏随机梯度估计器，避免了精确推理（如Viterbi算法）所需的O(|𝒴|²)二次复杂度。

Result: 理论证明LC Surrogates在全微分条件下严格保持线性H-一致性界。实验上：（1）在大词汇量序列标注任务中，相比结构化SVM实现23倍加速；（2）在带噪声的CIFAR-10数据集上，相比交叉熵提升2.6%的鲁棒性，对实例依赖标签噪声表现出优越的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: LC Surrogates成功统一了光滑损失和边际损失的优势：兼具光滑损失的优化便利性与边际损失的统计效率。该方法不仅理论上严格，而且在结构化预测和大规模分类任务中展现出显著的计算加速和鲁棒性提升，为损失函数设计提供了新的方向。

Original Abstract: The choice of loss function in classification involves a fundamental trade-off: smooth losses (like Cross-Entropy) enable fast optimization rates but yield slow square-root consistency bounds, while piecewise-linear losses (like Hinge) offer fast linear consistency rates but suffer from non-differentiability. We propose Linear-Core (LC) Surrogates, a new family of convex loss functions that resolve this tension by stitching a linear core to a smooth tail. We prove that these surrogates are differentiable everywhere while retaining strict linear $H$-consistency bounds, effectively combining the optimization benefits of smoothness with the statistical efficiency of margin-based losses. In the structured prediction setting, we show that this smoothness unlocks a massive computational and energy advantage: it allows for an unbiased stochastic gradient estimator that bypasses the quadratic complexity $O(|\mathscr{Y}|^2)$ of exact inference (e.g., Viterbi). Empirically, our method achieves a 23$\times$ speedup over Structured SVMs on large-vocabulary sequence tagging tasks and demonstrates superior robustness to instance-dependent label noise, outperforming Cross-Entropy by 2.6% on corrupted CIFAR-10.

中文摘要翻译: 分类中损失函数的选择涉及一个根本性权衡：光滑损失（如交叉熵）能够实现快速优化速率，但产生缓慢的平方根一致性界；而分段线性损失（如Hinge）提供快速的线性一致性界，但面临不可微的问题。我们提出Linear-Core (LC) Surrogates，一种新的凸损失函数族，通过将线性核心与平滑尾部拼接来解决这一矛盾。我们证明这些替代损失函数处处可微，同时严格保持线性H-一致性界，有效结合了光滑性的优化优势与基于边际损失的统计效率。在结构化预测设置中，我们展示了这种光滑性带来了巨大的计算和能量优势：它允许无偏随机梯度估计器绕过精确推理（如Viterbi）的二次复杂度O(|𝒴|²)。实验上，我们的方法在大词汇量序列标注任务上相比结构化SVM实现了23倍加速，并在带噪声的CIFAR-10数据集上展现出对实例依赖标签噪声的优越鲁棒性，比交叉熵提升2.6%。

Result: 在四个真实世界数据集上，CircuITS在联合密度估计和边缘密度估计方面均优于最先进的基线方法。

### [117] [CastFlow: Learning Role-Specialized Agentic Workflows for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27840)
*Bokai Pan,Mingyue Cheng,Zhiding Liu,Shuo Yu,Xiaoyu Tao,Yuchong Wu,Qi Liu,Defu Lian,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CastFlow 是一个动态智能体预测框架，通过多视角时序模式提取、多轮上下文获取、迭代预测优化和集成预测，克服了现有基于 LLM 的时序预测方法在静态生成范式下的局限性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于 LLM 的时序预测方法遵循静态生成范式，存在时序模式提取有限、单轮上下文获取、单次预测生成、缺乏集成预测支持等局限性，限制了预测性能。

Method: CastFlow 将预测过程组织为规划、行动、预测、反思四个阶段的智能体工作流，配备记忆模块和多视角工具包；采用角色专用设计，冻结通用 LLM 保持推理能力，微调领域专用 LLM 进行证据引导的数值预测；并开发了两阶段工作流导向训练（SFT + RLVR）。

Result: 在多种数据集上的大量实验表明，CastFlow 相比强基线方法取得了更优的综合结果。

Conclusion: CastFlow 作为一种动态智能体预测框架，在自适应性和准确性上超越了现有方法，为更自适应的时序预测迈出了重要一步。

Original Abstract: Recently, large language models (LLMs) have shown great promise in time series forecasting. However, most existing LLM-based forecasting methods still follow a static generative paradigm that directly maps historical observations to future values in a single pass. Under this paradigm, forecasting is constrained by limited temporal pattern extraction, single-round acquisition of contextual features, one-shot forecast generation, and lack of support from ensemble forecasts. To address these limitations, in this work, we propose CastFlow, a dynamic agentic forecasting framework that enables multi-view temporal pattern extraction, multi-round contextual features acquisition, iterative forecast refinement, and forecasting with ensemble forecasts. First, CastFlow organizes the forecasting process into planning, action, forecasting, and reflection, establishing an agentic workflow. Second, this workflow is supported by a memory module that retrieves prior experience and a multi-view toolkit that constructs diagnostic evidence and provides a reliable ensemble forecast baseline. Third, CastFlow adopts a role-specialized design that combines general-purpose reasoning with specialized numerical forecasting. Under this design, a frozen LLM preserves general-purpose reasoning, while a fine-tuned domain-specific LLM performs evidence-guided numerical forecasting based on the ensemble forecast baseline, rather than from scratch. To optimize a fine-tuned domain-specific LLM, we further develop a two-stage workflow-oriented training that combines supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). To evaluate the effectiveness of CastFlow, we conduct extensive experiments on diverse datasets and show that it achieves superior overall results against strong baselines. We hope that this work can serve as a step toward more adaptive and accurate time series forecasting.

中文摘要翻译: 近年来，大规模语言模型（LLMs）在时间序列预测中展现出巨大潜力。然而，现有基于LLM的预测方法大多仍遵循静态生成范式，即通过单次前向传播直接将历史观测映射到未来值。在该范式下，预测受到有限时序模式提取、单轮上下文特征获取、单次预测生成以及缺乏集成预测支持的限制。为解决这些局限，本文提出CastFlow——一个动态智能体预测框架，支持多视角时序模式提取、多轮上下文特征获取、迭代预测优化以及集成预测。首先，CastFlow将预测过程组织为规划、行动、预测和反思，构建了一个智能体工作流。其次，该工作流由检索先前经验的记忆模块和构建诊断证据并提供可靠集成预测基线的多视角工具包支撑。第三，CastFlow采用角色专用设计，将通用推理与专用数值预测相结合。在该设计下，冻结的LLM保留通用推理能力，而微调后的领域专用LLM在集成预测基线基础上进行证据引导的数值预测，而非从零开始。为优化微调的领域专用LLM，我们进一步开发了两阶段工作流导向训练，结合了监督微调（SFT）和基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）。为评估CastFlow的有效性，我们在多种数据集上进行了大量实验，结果表明其相比强基线方法取得了更优的综合结果。我们希望本工作能朝着更自适应、更准确的时间序列预测迈出一步。

</details>

Original Abstract: Animals hear and vocalize across frequency ranges that differ substantially from humans, often extending into the ultrasonic domain. Yet most computational bioacoustics systems rely on audio models pre-trained at 16 kHz, restricting their usable bandwidth to the 0-8 kHz baseband and discarding higher-frequency information present in many bioacoustic recordings. ### [119] [Differentiable latent structure discovery for interpretable forecasting in clinical time series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27967)
*Ivan Lerner,Jean Feydy,Alexandre Kalimouttou,Anita Burgun,Francis Bach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出StructGP和LP-StructGP，将过程卷积与可微结构学习结合，构建稀疏有向无环图，实现对不规则电子健康记录的连续时间、不确定性感知的多任务预测，在MIMIC-IV和PhysioNet数据集上验证了可解释性、良好校准性和可扩展性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法在处理不规则采样的电子健康记录时，要么需要插值到网格化数据从而损失信息，要么牺牲模型的可解释性，且缺乏对预测不确定性的合理量化，难以支持关键临床决策。

Method: StructGP是一种连续时间多任务高斯过程模型，通过过程卷积与可微结构学习联合优化，发现变量间稀疏有序的有向无环图；LP-StructGP在此基础上引入潜在路径，通过受试者特异性耦合滤波器和softmax门控机制捕获跨患者的共享时序演变模式；模型在稀疏性和无环约束下使用增广拉格朗日法和Adam优化器进行训练，并采用低秩更新保证可扩展性。

Result: 仿真实验表明模型能可靠恢复真实图结构（结构汉明距离趋近0）和路径分配（高调整兰德指数）。在MIMIC-IV脓毒症休克队列上，StructGP短时预测RMSE（0.68）优于独立任务基线（0.88）；增加15个输入后，校准覆盖率达0.96，远超非结构化核（0.84）。在PhysioNet挑战赛上，StructGP取得与最先进图神经模型相当的精度（MAE 3.72e-2），同时保持校准的不确定性。

Conclusion: 带有潜在路径的结构化过程卷积能够为不规则临床时间序列提供可解释、可扩展且具有良好校准不确定性的预测，为关键临床决策支持提供有效工具。

Original Abstract: Background: Timely, uncertainty-aware forecasting from irregular electronic health records (EHR) can support critical-care decisions, yet most approaches either impute to a grid or sacrifice interpretability. We introduce StructGP, a continuous-time multi-task Gaussian process that couples process convolutions with differentiable structure learning to uncover a sparse, ordered directed acyclic graph (DAG) of inter-variable dependencies while preserving principled uncertainty. We further propose LP-StructGP, which augments StructGP with latent pathways-shared, temporally shifted trajectories inferred via subject-specific coupling filters and a softmax gating mechanism-to capture cross-patient progression patterns. Both models are trained under sparsity and acyclicity constraints (augmented Lagrangian, Adam) using scalable low-rank updates. Results: In simulations, the approach reliably recovers ground-truth graphs (Structural Hamming Distance approaching 0 as cohorts grow) and pathway assignments (high Adjusted Rand Index). On a MIMIC-IV septic shock cohort (n=1,008; norepinephrine, creatinine, mean arterial pressure), StructGP improves short-horizon (6 h) forecasting over independent-task baselines (average RMSE 0.68 [95%CI: 0.63--0.74] vs. 0.88 [0.83-0.94]) and, with 15 additional inputs, markedly outperforms unstructured kernels (0.63 [0.58-0.69] vs. 3.02 [2.85-3.18]) with superior calibration (coverage 0.96 vs. 0.84). On the PhysioNet Challenge (12k patients, 41 variables), StructGP attains competitive accuracy (MAE 3.72e-2) relative to a state-of-the-art graph neural model while maintaining calibrated uncertainty. Conclusion: These results show that structured process convolutions with latent pathways deliver interpretable, scalable, and well-calibrated forecasting for irregular clinical time series.

中文摘要翻译: 背景：从不规则电子健康记录中进行及时且具有不确定性意识的预测能够支持关键临床决策，然而大多数方法要么需要插值到网格化数据，要么牺牲可解释性。本文提出StructGP，一种连续时间多任务高斯过程模型，它将过程卷积与可微结构学习相结合，以发现变量间稀疏、有序的有向无环图，同时保留原则性的不确定性量化。我们进一步提出LP-StructGP，该模型通过引入潜在路径——即通过受试者特异性耦合滤波器和softmax门控机制推断出的共享时序偏移轨迹——来捕获跨患者的进展模式。两种模型均在稀疏性和无环约束下（采用增广拉格朗日法和Adam优化器）通过可扩展的低秩更新进行训练。结果：在仿真实验中，该方法能够可靠地恢复真实图结构（结构汉明距离随队列规模增大趋近于0）和路径分配（高调整兰德指数）。在MIMIC-IV脓毒症休克队列（n=1,008；变量包括去甲肾上腺素、肌酐、平均动脉压）上，StructGP在短时域（6小时）预测中优于独立任务基线（平均RMSE 0.68 [95%CI: 0.63–0.74] vs. 0.88 [0.83–0.94]），且在额外输入15个变量后，其表现显著优于非结构化核（0.63 [0.58–0.69] vs. 3.02 [2.85–3.18]），并具有更优的校准性能（覆盖度0.96 vs. 0.84）。在PhysioNet挑战数据集（12,000名患者，41个变量）上，StructGP取得了与最先进的图神经模型相当的预测精度（MAE 3.72e-2），同时保持了校准良好的不确定性估计。结论：这些结果表明，结合潜在路径的结构化过程卷积能够为不规则的临床时间序列提供可解释、可扩展且具有良好校准不确定性的预测。

</details>


### [120] [ITS-Mina: A Harris Hawks Optimization-Based All-MLP Framework with Iterative Refinement and External Attention for Multivariate Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27981)
*Pourya Zamanvaziri,Amirhossein Sadr,Aida Pakniyat,Dara Rahmati*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ITS-Mina是一个全MLP框架，通过迭代精炼机制、外部注意力模块和HHO自适应正则化，在多变量时间序列预测中达到SOTA性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: Transformer在时间序列预测中计算开销大，而MLP模型性能可与Transformer匹敌且更高效，因此探索更优的MLP架构。

Method: (1) 迭代精炼机制：共享参数的残差混合器堆栈逐步增强时序表示；(2) 外部注意力模块：用可学习记忆单元替代自注意力，线性复杂度捕获跨样本全局依赖；(3) HHO算法自动调优dropout率，实现自适应正则化。

Result: 在6个基准数据集上与11个基线模型对比，ITS-Mina在多个预测视域上达到SOTA或极具竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的全MLP框架ITS-Mina在保持低计算成本的同时，通过三项创新设计显著提升了多变量时间序列预测性能。

Original Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting plays a pivotal role in numerous real-world applications, including financial analysis, energy management, and traffic planning. While Transformer-based architectures have gained popularity for this task, recent studies reveal that simpler MLP-based models can achieve competitive or superior performance with significantly reduced computational cost. In this paper, we propose ITS-Mina, a novel all-MLP framework for multivariate time series forecasting that integrates three key innovations: (1) an iterative refinement mechanism that progressively enhances temporal representations by repeatedly applying a shared-parameter residual mixer stack, effectively deepening the model's computational capacity without multiplying the number of distinct parameters; (2) an external attention module that replaces traditional self-attention with learnable memory units, capturing cross-sample global dependencies at linear computational complexity; and (3) a Harris Hawks Optimization (HHO) algorithm for automatic dropout rate tuning, enabling adaptive regularization tailored to each dataset. Extensive experiments on six widely-used benchmark datasets demonstrate that ITS-Mina achieves state-of-the-art or highly competitive performance compared to eleven baseline models across multiple forecasting horizons.

中文摘要翻译: 多变量时间序列预测在金融分析、能源管理和交通规划等众多实际应用中扮演着关键角色。尽管基于Transformer的架构在该任务中广受欢迎，但近期研究表明，更简单的基于MLP的模型能够以显著降低的计算成本实现具有竞争力甚至更优的性能。本文提出ITS-Mina，一种新颖的全MLP多变量时间序列预测框架，该框架融合了三项关键创新：(1) 迭代精炼机制，通过重复应用共享参数的残差混合器堆栈逐步增强时序表示，有效加深模型的计算容量而不增加独立参数数量；(2) 外部注意力模块，用可学习记忆单元替代传统自注意力机制，以线性计算复杂度捕获跨样本全局依赖关系；(3) Harris Hawks优化(HHO)算法用于自动调节dropout率，实现对每个数据集量身定制的自适应正则化。在六个广泛使用的基准数据集上的大量实验表明，ITS-Mina在多个预测视域上与十一个基线模型相比，达到了最优或极具竞争力的性能。

### [121] [Dynamic Scaled Gradient Descent for Stable Fine-Tuning for Classifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27987)
*Nghia Bui,Lijing Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出动态缩放梯度下降（DSGD）算法，通过动态缩放正确分类样本的梯度来防止梯度抵消，从而提高微调预训练模型时的训练稳定性和性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 微调预训练模型时，模型容易陷入坍塌状态（collapsed state），导致性能下降和训练不稳定。一个可能原因是不同训练样本的梯度相互抵消。现有方法对此问题缺乏有效解决手段。

Method: 提出动态缩放梯度下降（DSGD）算法，在训练过程中直接修改每个训练样本返回的梯度，具体做法是利用动态缩放因子降低被正确分类样本的梯度贡献。

Result: 在多种基准数据集、多个任务和大型预训练模型上的实验表明，该方法能持续降低性能方差，并在准确率上超过现有方法。

Conclusion: DSGD算法通过动态缩放正确分类样本的梯度，在理论和实践上均能有效提升训练稳定性，并取得更优的准确率表现。

Original Abstract: Fine-tuning pretrained models has become a standard approach to adapting pretrained knowledge to improve the accuracy on new sparse, imbalance datasets. However, issues arise when optimization falls into a collapsed state, where the model gets stuck, leading to degraded performance and unstable training. One possible reason for this is the cancellation of gradients across training examples. To address this problem, we propose a novel algorithm, dynamic scaled gradient descent (\mName), that directly modifies the gradients returned by training examples, specifically, scaling down the gradients of correctly classified examples using a dynamic scaler. This strategy offers both theoretical and empirical advantages in improving training stability. Experiments on a variety of benchmark datasets, spanning multiple tasks and large pretrained models, demonstrate that our method consistently reduces performance variance and surpasses the accuracy of existing approaches.

中文摘要翻译: 微调预训练模型已成为一种标准方法，用于调整预训练知识以提高在新稀疏、不平衡数据集上的准确性。然而，当优化陷入坍塌状态（模型停滞不前）时，会出现性能下降和训练不稳定等问题。一个可能的原因是不同训练样本之间的梯度相互抵消。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了一种新颖的算法——动态缩放梯度下降（DSGD），它直接修改训练样本返回的梯度，具体而言，使用动态缩放因子降低正确分类样本的梯度。该策略在提升训练稳定性方面具有理论和实践上的双重优势。在涵盖多种任务和大型预训练模型的多个基准数据集上的实验表明，我们的方法能够持续降低性能方差，并在准确率上超越现有方法。

</details>


### [122] [Learning from Disagreement: Clinician Overrides as Implicit Preference Signals for Clinical AI in Value-Based Care](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28010)
*Prabhjot Singh,Abhishek Gupta,Chris Betz,Abe Flansburg,Brett Ives,Sudeep Lama,Jung Hoon Son*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将临床医生对AI建议的否决行为重构为隐式偏好数据，扩展了RLHF框架，引入五类否决分类法、基于状态的偏好公式和双学习架构来解决抑制偏差问题，并在基于价值的医疗场景中验证。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 临床医生常否决AI建议，这些否决行为蕴含丰富的领域专家偏好信息，但未被系统用于模型改进。现有RLHF方法在医疗场景中面临抑制偏差——当临床医生能力不足时，正确但困难的建议被系统性压制。

Method: 提出三部分框架：(1) 五类否决分类法，将否决类型映射为不同模型更新目标；(2) 基于患者状态s、组织语境c和临床医生能力κ的偏好公式，其中κ分解为执行能力κ_exec和对齐能力κ_align；(3) 双学习架构，通过交替优化联合训练奖励模型和能力模型，防止抑制偏差。

Result: 慢性病管理在按结果付费合同下产生的否决数据具有纵向密度高、决策空间集中、有结果标签、能力自然变化等有利特性；结合纵向结果测量和财务激励的训练环境是学习与患者轨迹而非就诊经济对齐的奖励模型的必要条件。

Conclusion: 临床否决数据可作为隐式偏好信号用于改进AI模型，但需处理抑制偏差；双学习架构和适当的激励环境是释放这一数据价值的关键。该框架已在真实价值医疗部署中得到验证。

Original Abstract: We reframe clinician overrides of clinical AI recommendations as implicit preference data - the same signal structure exploited by reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), but richer: the annotator is a domain expert, the alternatives carry real consequences, and downstream outcomes are observable. We present a formal framework extending standard preference learning with three contributions: a five-category override taxonomy mapping override types to distinct model update targets; a preference formulation conditioned on patient state s, organizational context c, and clinician capability kappa, where kappa decomposes into execution capability kappa-exec and alignment capability kappa-align; and a dual learning architecture that jointly trains a reward model and a capability model via alternating optimization, preventing a failure mode we term suppression bias-the systematic suppression of correct-but-difficult recommendations when clinician capability falls below the execution threshold. We argue that chronic disease management under outcome-based payment contracts produces override data with uniquely favorable properties-longitudinal density, concentrated decision space, outcome labels, and natural capability variation-and that training environments combining longitudinal outcome measurement with aligned financial incentives are a necessary condition for learning a reward model aligned with patient trajectory rather than with encounter economics. This framework emerged from operational work to improve clinician capability in a live value-based care deployment.

中文摘要翻译: 我们将临床医生对临床AI推荐的否决行为重构为隐式偏好数据——其信号结构与基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）所利用的相同，但更为丰富：注释者是领域专家，备选方案具有真实后果，且下游结果可观测。我们提出了一个形式化框架，通过三项贡献扩展了标准偏好学习：一个五类否决分类法，将否决类型映射到不同的模型更新目标；一个基于患者状态s、组织语境c和临床医生能力κ的条件偏好公式，其中κ分解为执行能力κ_exec和对齐能力κ_align；以及一个双学习架构，通过交替优化联合训练奖励模型和能力模型，防止我们称之为抑制偏差的失败模式——即当临床医生能力低于执行阈值时，正确但困难的推荐被系统性压制。我们认为，在按结果付费合同下的慢性病管理所产生的否决数据具有独特的有利特性——纵向密度、集中的决策空间、结果标签和自然的能力变化——并且将纵向结果测量与对齐的财务激励相结合的训练环境，是学习与患者轨迹对齐而非与就诊经济对齐的奖励模型的必要条件。该框架源于在真实价值医疗部署中为提升临床医生能力而开展的运营工作。

### [123] [Cost-Aware Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28020)
*Clara Mohri,Amir Globerson,Haim Kaplan,Tomer Koren,Yishay Mansour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对代价感知学习问题，提出了代价感知SGD算法并推导了其代价复杂度，建立了理论下界，并将该方法应用于语言模型强化学习中的策略优化，提出了Cost-Aware GRPO算法，在1.5B和8B LLM上实现了约30%的token减少且性能不降。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在有限和优化问题中，不同组件函数的采样代价不同，现有方法忽视了这一代价差异，导致资源浪费。本文旨在设计一种能在达到目标误差的同时最小化总代价的优化算法。

Method: 1) 提出代价感知SGD算法，针对凸函数推导代价复杂度；2) 建立该设置下的理论下界；3) 提出子集选择算法进一步降低训练代价；4) 将理论应用于语言模型强化学习，提出Cost-Aware GRPO算法，根据序列长度调整策略梯度的计算代价。

Result: 在1.5B和8B规模的语言模型上，Cost-Aware GRPO可将策略优化中使用的token数减少约30%，同时匹配或超越基线准确率。

Conclusion: 代价感知学习能够有效降低训练成本，理论分析和实验验证均表明该方法在保持性能的同时显著节约资源，尤其适用于序列长度差异大的语言模型强化学习场景。

Original Abstract: We consider the problem of Cost-Aware Learning, where sampling different component functions of a finite-sum objective incurs different costs. The objective is to reach a target error while minimizing the total cost. First, we propose the Cost-Aware Stochastic Gradient Descent algorithm for convex functions, and derive its cost complexity to attain an error of $ε$. Furthermore, we establish a lower bound for this setting and provide a subset selection algorithm to further reduce the cost of training. We apply our theoretical insights to reinforcement learning with language models, where the computational cost of policy gradients varies with sequence length. To this end, we introduce Cost-Aware GRPO, an algorithm designed to reduce the cost of policy optimization while preserving performance. Empirical results on 1.5B and 8B LLMs demonstrate that our approach reduces the tokens used in policy optimization by up to about 30% while matching or exceeding baseline accuracy.

中文摘要翻译: 我们考虑了代价感知学习问题，其中对有限和目标函数中不同组件函数进行采样的代价各不相同。目标是在最小化总代价的同时达到目标误差。首先，我们针对凸函数提出了代价感知随机梯度下降算法，并推导了其达到ε误差所需的代价复杂度。此外，我们为该设置建立了理论下界，并提出了一种子集选择算法以进一步降低训练代价。我们将理论见解应用于语言模型强化学习，其中策略梯度的计算代价随序列长度变化。为此，我们引入了Cost-Aware GRPO，一种旨在降低策略优化代价同时保持性能的算法。在1.5B和8B大语言模型上的实验结果表明，我们的方法可将策略优化中使用的token数减少约30%，同时匹配或超越基线准确率。

### [124] [FedHarmony: Harmonizing Heterogeneous Label Correlations in Federated Multi-Label Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28024)
*Zhiqiang Kou,Junxiang Wu,Wenke Huang,Wenwen He,Ming-Kun Xie,Changwei Wang,Yuheng Jia,Di Jiang,Yang Liu,Xin Geng,Qiang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedHarmony提出了一种联邦多标签学习框架，通过共识相关性校准客户端本地标签偏差，并设计基于数据量和相关性质量的加权聚合策略，同时开发了加速优化算法，在保护隐私的前提下有效处理异质标签分布下的标签相关性漂移问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在联邦多标签学习中，不同客户端拥有异质的标签空间和共现模式，导致各客户端学到的标签相关性偏离全局结构（即标签相关性漂移），现有方法难以在此类异质分布下准确建模全局标签相关性。

Method: 提出FedHarmony框架：1）引入共识相关性，将其作为全局教师来纠正客户端的局部有偏估计；2）聚合时综合考虑数据量和相关性质量进行加权；3）开发加速优化算法，在保证精度的同时实现更快的收敛。

Result: 在真实联邦多标签数据集上，FedHarmony持续优于现有最先进方法；同时从理论上证明了其加速优化算法的更快收敛性且不牺牲精度。

Conclusion: FedHarmony通过协调异质客户端间的标签相关性，有效解决了标签相关性漂移问题，兼顾了隐私保护、通信效率和模型性能。

Original Abstract: Federated Multi-Label Learning is a distributed paradigm where multiple clients possess heterogeneous multi-label data and perform collaborative learning under privacy constraints without sharing raw data. However, modeling label correlations under heterogeneous distributions remains challenging. Due to client-specific label spaces and varying co-occurrence patterns, correlations learned by individual clients inevitably deviate from the global structure, a phenomenon we term label correlation drift. To address this, we propose FedHarmony, a framework that harmonizes heterogeneous label correlations across clients. It introduces consensus correlation, capturing agreement among other clients and serving as a global teacher to correct biased local estimates. During aggregation, FedHarmony evaluates each client by both data size and correlation quality, assigning weights accordingly. Moreover, we develop an accelerated optimization algorithm for FedHarmony and theoretically establish faster convergence without sacrificing accuracy. Experiments on real-world federated multi-label datasets show that FedHarmony consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦多标签学习是一种分布式学习范式，其中多个客户端拥有异质的多标签数据，在隐私约束下进行协作学习而不共享原始数据。然而，在异质分布下建模标签相关性仍然具有挑战性。由于客户端特有的标签空间和不同的共现模式，各个客户端学习到的相关性不可避免地偏离全局结构，我们将这一现象称为标签相关性漂移。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了FedHarmony，一个用于协调跨客户端异质标签相关性的框架。它引入了共识相关性，捕捉其他客户端间的共识并作为全局教师来纠正有偏的局部估计。在聚合过程中，FedHarmony根据数据量和相关性质量对每个客户端进行评估并赋予相应权重。此外，我们为FedHarmony开发了一种加速优化算法，并从理论上证明了其在不牺牲精度的情况下实现更快的收敛。在真实联邦多标签数据集上的实验表明，FedHarmony持续优于现有最先进方法。

### [125] [MIFair: A Mutual-Information Framework for Intersectionality and Multiclass Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28030)
*Jeanne Monnier,Thomas George,Frédéric Guyard,Christèle Tarnec,Marios Kountouris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出MIFair，一个基于互信息的统一公平性评估与缓解框架。它提供灵活度量模板和基于正则化的训练方法，天然支持交叉性、多属性子群和多分类场景，在多个表格和图像数据集上有效降低偏差且保持强预测性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有公平性方法在交叉性、多分类设置、灵活性和通用性方面仍存在不足，缺乏统一的框架来整合不同的公平性要求。

Method: 基于互信息（Mutual Information）构建统一的公平性度量模板和预处理缓解方法。受Prejudice Remover启发，将群体公平性定义为预测派生变量与敏感属性之间的统计独立性，并通过正则化训练减少偏差。理论层面建立与独立性（Independence）和分离性（Separation）等经典公平性概念的等价关系。

Result: 在真实世界的表格和图像数据集上的实验表明，MIFair有效降低偏差（包括此前未解决的多元属性场景），同时在评估设置中保持强预测性能。

Conclusion: MIFair作为一个统一框架，整合了多种公平性需求，支持一致的基准测试并简化实际使用，为公平性机器学习提供了信息论视角下的灵活通用解决方案。

Original Abstract: Fairness in machine learning remains challenging due to its ethical complexity, the absence of a universal definition, and the need for context-specific bias metrics. Existing methods still struggle with intersectionality, multiclass settings, and limited flexibility and generality. To address these gaps, we introduce MIFair, a unified framework for bias assessment and mitigation based on mutual information. MIFair provides a flexible metric template and an in-processing mitigation method inspired by the Prejudice Remover, defining group fairness as statistical independence between prediction-derived variables and sensitive attributes. We further strengthen its information-theoretic foundation by establishing equivalences with widely used fairness notions such as independence and separation. MIFair naturally supports intersectionality, complex subgroup structures, and multiclass classification and employs regularization-based training to reduce bias according to the selected metric. Its key advantage is its versatility: it consolidates diverse fairness requirements into a single coherent framework, enabling consistent benchmarking and simplifying practical use. Experiments on real-world tabular and image datasets show that MIFair effectively reduces bias, including previously unaddressed multi-attribute scenarios, while maintaining strong predictive performance across the evaluated settings.

中文摘要翻译: 机器学习中的公平性因其伦理复杂性、缺乏统一定义以及需要特定上下文的偏差度量而仍然具有挑战性。现有方法在交叉性、多分类设置以及有限灵活性和通用性方面仍存在不足。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了MIFair，一个基于互信息的偏差评估与缓解的统一框架。MIFair提供了一个灵活的度量模板和一种受偏见消除器（Prejudice Remover）启发的处理中缓解方法，将群体公平性定义为预测派生变量与敏感属性之间的统计独立性。我们进一步通过建立与广泛使用的公平性概念（如独立性和分离性）的等价关系，强化了其信息论基础。MIFair天然支持交叉性、复杂子群结构和多分类任务，并采用基于正则化的训练来根据所选度量减少偏差。其关键优势在于通用性：它将多样化的公平性需求整合到单一连贯框架中，从而实现一致的基准测试并简化实际使用。在真实世界的表格和图像数据集上的实验表明，MIFair有效降低了偏差（包括此前未解决的多元属性场景），同时在评估的设置中保持了强预测性能。

</details>


### [126] [Shuffling-Aware Optimization for Private Vector Mean Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28032)
*Shun Takagi,Seng Pei Liew*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了单消息混洗模型下的d维无偏均值估计问题，提出了混洗指数（shuffle index）来形式化后混洗机制设计，建立了基于混洗指数的极小化极大下界，并构造了在高隐私预算下渐近最优的机制，该机制能达到与中心化高斯机制几乎相同的隐私-效用权衡。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 局部差分隐私（LDP）下的极小化极大最优机制已被充分研究，但混洗后（post-shuffling）的最优性概念尚未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究单消息混洗模型中均值估计的最优机制设计问题。

Method: 引入混洗指数（shuffle index），将后混洗机制设计问题形式化为一个显式优化问题；建立基于混洗指数的极小化极大均方误差下界；在高隐私预算下构造渐近极小化极大最优机制。

Result: （1）建立了基于混洗指数的极小化极大均方误差下界；（2）证明LDP下最优的机制在混洗后可能变得次优；（3）构造的渐近最优机制在隐私-效用权衡上几乎等同于中心化高斯机制。

Conclusion: 混洗可以改变隐私-效用权衡的结构，LDP最优机制在混洗后不再保持最优；通过混洗指数可以系统性地设计后混洗最优机制，且在高隐私预算下能达到与中心化高斯机制几乎相同的性能。

Original Abstract: We study $d$-dimensional unbiased mean estimation in the single-message shuffle model, where each user sends a single privatized message and the analyzer only observes the shuffled multiset of reports. While minimax-optimal mechanisms are well understood in the local differential privacy setting, the corresponding notion of optimality after shuffling has remained largely unexplored. To address this gap, we introduce the recently proposed shuffle index and use it to formulate the post-shuffling mechanism design problem as an explicit optimization problem. We then establish a minimax lower bound on the achievable mean squared error in terms of the shuffle index, which implies that mechanisms that are optimal under LDP can become suboptimal once shuffling is applied. Finally, we construct an asymptotically minimax optimal mechanism in the high privacy regime, which as a consequence achieves a privacy-utility trade-off nearly identical to that of the central Gaussian mechanism.

中文摘要翻译: 我们研究了单消息混洗模型中的$d$维无偏均值估计问题，在该模型中，每个用户发送一条私有化消息，分析器仅能观察到报告的混洗后多重集。虽然在局部差分隐私设置下极小化极大最优机制已被充分理解，但混洗后相应的最优性概念在很大程度上仍未得到探索。为填补这一空白，我们引入了近期提出的混洗指数，并利用它将后混洗机制设计问题形式化为一个显式优化问题。随后，我们基于混洗指数建立了可达均方误差的极小化极大下界，这表明在LDP下最优的机制在应用混洗后可能变得次优。最后，我们在高隐私预算下构造了一个渐近极小化极大最优机制，其隐私-效用权衡几乎与中心化高斯机制相同。

### [127] [Exponential families from a single KL identity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28036)
*Marc Dymetman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从指数族分布中一个简单恒等式出发，结合KL散度非负性，通过纯代数推导统一得到了多个经典结果，包括三标识恒等式、I-投影和逆I-投影的勾股定理、对数配分函数的凸性、其Legendre对偶的KL表示、Gibbs变分原理以及KL正则化奖励最大化中的显式优化器（指数倾斜公式），无需传统上各自独立的繁复论证。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 指数族分布是现代机器学习（softmax、高斯、玻尔兹曼分布）的核心，也是变分推断、熵正则化强化学习和RLHF的理论基础。现有方法对相关结果（如勾股定理、变分原理等）需要各自独立的繁复推导，缺乏统一视角。本文旨在通过一个简单恒等式统一这些经典结果，简化理论推导。

Method: 作者从指数族中一个关于KL散度差的对数配分函数-矩恒等式出发，仅结合KL散度非负性（且等号成立当且仅当分布相等），通过直接代入和代数重排（纯代数操作），推导出一系列经典结论。此外，辅以标准分析论证恢复梯度公式、Bregman表示的KL散度以及矩映射的满射性。

Result: 推导得到了以下结果的统一证明：广义三标识恒等式、I-投影和逆I-投影的勾股定理、对数配分函数A(λ)的凸性、其Legendre对偶的KL散度表示、Gibbs变分原理、KL正则化奖励最大化中的显式优化器（指数倾斜公式），以及对数配分函数的梯度公式、族内KL散度的Bregman表示和矩映射的满射性。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，指数族中一个简单的恒等式与KL散度非负性相结合，足以以统一且简洁的方式导出多个原本需要独立繁复论证的经典结果，为该领域提供了一种自洽且优雅的理论框架。

Original Abstract: Exponential families encompass the distributions central to modern machine learning -- softmax, Gaussians, and Boltzmann distributions -- and underlie the theory of variational inference, entropy-regularized reinforcement learning, and RLHF. We isolate a simple identity for exponential families that expresses the KL difference $\mathrm{KL}(q \| p_{λ_2}) - \mathrm{KL}(q \| p_{λ_1})$ in terms of the log-partition function $A(λ)$ and the moment $μ_q$. Remarkably, this identity together with the single fact that $\mathrm{KL} \geq 0$ (with equality iff $p = q$) suffices, by direct substitution and rearrangement, to derive a cluster of results that are classically obtained by separate, heavier arguments: a generalized three-point identity for arbitrary reference distributions, Pythagorean theorems for I-projections and reverse I-projections, convexity of the log-partition function, identification of its Legendre dual in KL terms, the Gibbs variational principle, and the explicit optimizer in KL-regularized reward maximization, including the exponential tilting formula underlying entropy-regularized control and RLHF. Beyond these purely algebraic consequences, standard analytic arguments recover the gradient formula for the log-partition function, the Bregman representation of within-family KL divergence, and the surjectivity of the moment map. The note is self-contained.

中文摘要翻译: 指数族涵盖了现代机器学习中核心的分布——softmax、高斯分布和玻尔兹曼分布——并且是变分推断、熵正则化强化学习以及基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）的理论基础。我们分离出指数族的一个简单恒等式，该恒等式将KL散度差 $\mathrm{KL}(q \| p_{λ_2}) - \mathrm{KL}(q \| p_{λ_1})$ 用对数配分函数 $A(λ)$ 和矩 $μ_q$ 表示。值得注意的是，该恒等式结合 $\mathrm{KL} \geq 0$（等号成立当且仅当 $p = q$）这一单一事实，通过直接代入和重排，即可推导出一系列经典结果，而这些结果传统上需要各自独立的繁复论证：适用于任意参考分布的广义三标识恒等式、I-投影和逆I-投影的勾股定理、对数配分函数的凸性、其Legendre对偶在KL散度项下的识别、Gibbs变分原理，以及KL正则化奖励最大化中的显式优化器——包括支撑熵正则化控制和RLHF的指数倾斜公式。除这些纯代数推论外，标准分析论证还可恢复对数配分函数的梯度公式、族内KL散度的Bregman表示以及矩映射的满射性。本文是自包含的。

### [128] [Early Detection of Water Stress by Plant Electrophysiology: Machine Learning for Irrigation Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28038)
*Eduard Buss,Till Aust,Heiko Hamann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于机器学习的框架，利用植物电生理信号在线检测番茄植株的水分胁迫，可在30分钟时间窗口内实现高达92%的分类准确率，为精准农业中的智能灌溉控制提供决策支持。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 快速检测植物胁迫是实现植物表型分析、精准农业和自动化作物管理的关键，尤其是在灌溉管理方面，需要早期识别水分胁迫以优化资源利用并维持作物产量，而直接生理传感可在可见症状出现前检测胁迫响应。

Method: 记录温室番茄植株在水分胁迫下的电生理信号，构建基于机器学习的在线胁迫检测框架。处理流程包括：统计特征提取与选择、自动化机器学习（AutoML）或深度学习、以及概率校准。

Result: 30分钟回溯窗口在决策速度与分类性能之间取得最佳平衡；自动化机器学习分类准确率高达92%，优于深度学习方法；序列后向选择在保持性能的同时减少了特征集；框架能够检测从健康到胁迫状态的转变，且能泛化到训练集未包含的记录。

Conclusion: 该工作为农民提供了决策支持工具，并为基于生物反馈的灌溉控制奠定基础，有助于提高（半）自动化作物生产系统的资源利用效率。

Original Abstract: Purpose: Fast detection of plant stress is key to plant phenotyping, precision agriculture, and automated crop management. In particular, efficient irrigation management requires early identification of water stress to optimize resource use while maintaining crop performance. Direct physiological sensing offers the potential to detect stress responses before visible symptoms appear. Methods: In this study, we recorded electrophysiological signals from greenhouse-grown tomato plants subjected to water stress and developed a framework based on machine learning for online stress detection. The recorded time-series data were processed using a processing pipeline that includes statistical feature extraction and selection, automated machine learning or alternatively deep learning, and probability calibration. Results: Across multiple input time horizons, we found that a 30-minute look-back window strikes the best balance between rapid decision-making and classification performance. Using automated machine learning, the framework achieved classification accuracies of up to 92%, outperforming deep learning approaches. Sequential backward selection reduced the feature set while maintaining performance. Importantly, the framework detects transitions from healthy to stressed states in recordings that were not included in the training set. Conclusion: Overall, we provide a decision-support tool for farmers and establish a foundation for biofeedback-driven irrigation control to improve resource efficiency in (semi-)autonomous crop production systems.

中文摘要翻译: 目的：快速检测植物胁迫是植物表型分析、精准农业和自动化作物管理的关键。特别是，有效的灌溉管理需要早期识别水分胁迫，以在维持作物性能的同时优化资源利用。直接生理传感能够在可见症状出现之前检测胁迫响应。方法：在本研究中，我们记录了受到水分胁迫的温室番茄植株的电生理信号，并开发了一个基于机器学习的在线胁迫检测框架。记录的时序数据通过一个处理流程进行加工，该流程包括统计特征提取与选择、自动化机器学习或深度学习，以及概率校准。结果：在多个输入时间窗口上，我们发现30分钟的回溯窗口在快速决策与分类性能之间取得了最佳平衡。使用自动化机器学习，该框架的分类准确率高达92%，优于深度学习方法。序列后向选择在保持性能的同时减少了特征集。重要的是，该框架能够检测训练集未包含的记录中从健康到胁迫状态的转变。结论：总体而言，我们为农民提供了一个决策支持工具，并为基于生物反馈的灌溉控制奠定了基础，以提高（半）自动化作物生产系统的资源利用效率。
